وقد اختلف النحاة في قوله: ﴿مِنْ قَبْلِ أَنْ يُنزلَ عَلَيْهِمْ مِنْ قَبْلِهِ لَمُبْلِسِينَ﴾ ، فقال ابن جرير: هو تَأْكِيدٌ. وَحَكَاهُ عَنْ بَعْضِ أَهْلِ الْعَرَبِيَّةِ.

وَقَالَ آخَرُونَ: [وَإِنْ كَانُوا] مِنْ قَبْلِ أَنْ يُنَزَّلَ عَلَيْهِمُ الْمَطَرُ، ﴿مِنْ قَبْلِهِ﴾ أَيِ: الْإِنْزَالِ ﴿لَمُبْلِسِينَ﴾ .

وَيُحْتَمَلُ أَنْ يَكُونَ ذَلِكَ مِنْ دَلَالَةِ التَّأْسِيسِ، وَيَكُونُ مَعْنَى الْكَلَامِ: أَنَّهُمْ كَانُوا مُحْتَاجِينَ إِلَيْهِ قَبِلَ نُزُولِهِ، وَمِنْ قَبْلِهِ -أَيْضًا -قَدْ فَاتَ عِنْدَهُمْ نُزُولُهُ وَقْتًا بَعْدَ وَقْتٍ، فَتَرَقَّبُوهُ فِي إِبَّانِهِ فَتَأَخَّرَ، فَمَضَتْ مُدَّةٌ فَتَرَقَّبُوهُ فَتَأَخَّرَ، ثُمَّ جَاءَهُمْ بَغْتَةً بَعْدَ الْإِيَاسِ مِنْهُ وَالْقُنُوطِ، فَبَعْدَ مَا كَانَتْ أَرْضُهُمْ مُقَشْعَرَةً هَامِدَةً أَصْبَحَتْ وَقَدِ اهتزت وربت، وأنبتت من كل زوج بهيج؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿فَانْظُرْ إِلَى آثَارِ رَحْمَةِ اللَّهِ﴾ يَعْنِي: الْمَطَرَ ﴿كَيْفَ يُحْيِي الأرْضَ بَعْدَ مَوْتِهَا﴾ .

ثُمَّ نَبَّهَ بِذَلِكَ عَلَى إِحْيَاءِ الْأَجْسَادِ بَعْدَ مَوْتِهَا وَتَفَرُّقِهَا وَتَمَزُّقِهَا، فَقَالَ: ﴿إِنَّ ذَلِكَ لَمُحْيِي الْمَوْتَى﴾ أَيْ: إِنَّ الَّذِي فَعَلَ ذَلِكَ لَقَادِرٌ عَلَى إِحْيَاءِ الْأَمْوَاتِ، ﴿إنَّهُ عَلَى كُلِّ شَيْءٍ قَدِيرٌ﴾ .

ثُمَّ قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَئِنْ أَرْسَلْنَا رِيحًا فَرَأَوْهُ مُصْفَرًّا لَظَلُّوا مِنْ بَعْدِهِ يَكْفُرُونَ﴾ ، يَقُولُ ﴿وَلَئِنْ أَرْسَلْنَا رِيحًا﴾ يَابِسَةً عَلَى الزَّرْعِ الَّذِي زَرَعُوهُ، وَنَبَتَ وَشَبَّ وَاسْتَوَى عَلَى سُوقِهِ، فَرَأَوْهُ مُصْفَرًّا، أَيْ: قَدِ اصْفَرَّ وَشَرَعَ فِي الْفَسَادِ، لَظَلُّوا مِنْ بَعْدِهِ، أَيْ: بَعْدَ هَذَا الْحَالِ يَكْفُرُونَ، أَيْ: يَجْحَدُونَ مَا تَقَدَّمَ [إِلَيْهِمْ] مِنَ النِّعَمِ، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿أَفَرَأَيْتُمْ مَا تَحْرُثُونَ أَأَنْتُمْ تَزْرَعُونَهُ أَمْ نَحْنُ الزَّارِعُونَ. لَوْ نَشَاءُ لَجَعَلْنَاهُ حُطَامًا فَظَلْتُمْ تَفَكَّهُونَ. إِنَّا لَمُغْرَمُونَ بَلْ نَحْنُ مَحْرُومُونَ﴾ [الْوَاقِعَةِ: ٦٣ -٦٧] .

قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا محمد بن عيسى بن الطباع، حَدَّثَنَا هُشَيْم ، عَنْ يَعْلَى بْنِ عَطَاءٍ، عَنِ أَبِيهِ عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمْرٍو، قَالَ: الرِّيَاحُ ثَمَانِيَةٌ، أَرْبَعَةٌ مِنْهَا رَحْمَةٌ، وَأَرْبَعَةٌ عَذَابٌ، فَأَمَّا الرَّحْمَةُ فَالنَّاشِرَاتُ وَالْمُبَشِّرَاتُ وَالْمُرْسَلَاتُ وَالذَّارِيَاتُ. وَأَمَّا الْعَذَابُ فَالْعَقِيمُ وَالصَّرْصَرُ، وَهُمَا فِي الْبَرِّ، وَالْعَاصِفُ وَالْقَاصِفُ، وَهُمَا فِي الْبَحْرِ [فَإِذَا شَاءَ سُبْحَانَهُ وَتَعَالَى حَرَّكَهُ بِحَرَكَةِ الرَّحْمَةِ فَجَعَلَهُ رَخَاءً وَرَحْمَةً وَبُشْرَى بَيْنَ يَدَيْ رحْمته، وَلَاقِحًا لِلسَّحَابِ تُلَقِّحُهُ بِحَمْلِهِ الْمَاءَ، كَمَا يُلَقِّحُ الذَّكَرُ الْأُنْثَى بِالْحَمْلِ، وَإِنْ شَاءَ حَرَّكَهُ بِحَرَكَةِ الْعَذَابِ فَجَعَلَهُ عَقِيمًا، وَأَوْدَعَهُ عَذَابًا أَلِيمًا، وَجَعْلَهُ نِقْمَةً عَلَى مَنْ يَشَاءُ مِنْ عِبَادِهِ، فَيَجْعَلُهُ صَرْصَرًا وَعَاتِيًا وَمُفْسِدًا لِمَا يَمُرُّ عَلَيْهِ، وَالرِّيَاحُ مُخْتَلِفَةٌ فِي مَهَابِّهَا: صَبًا وَدَبُورٌ، وَجَنُوبٌ، وَشِمَالٌ، وَفِي مَنْفَعَتِهَا وَتَأْثِيرِهَا أَعْظَمَ اخْتِلَافِ، فَرِيحٌ لَيِّنَةٌ رَطْبَةٌ تُغَذِّي النَّبَاتَ وَأَبْدَانَ الْحَيَوَانِ، وَأُخْرَى تُجَفِّفُهُ، وَأُخْرَى تُهْلِكُهُ وَتُعْطِبُهُ، وَأُخْرَى تُسَيِّرُهُ وَتَصْلُبُهُ، وَأُخْرَى تُوهِنُهُ وَتُضْعِفُهُ] .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو عبُيَد اللَّهِ ابْنِ أَخِي ابْنِ وَهْبٍ، حَدَّثَنَا عَمِّي، حدثنا عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ عَيْاش ، حَدَّثَنِي عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ سُلَيْمَانَ، عَنْ دَرَّاجٍ، عَنْ عِيسَى بْنِ هِلَالٍ الصدَفي، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمْرٍو قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "الرِّيحُ مُسَخَّرَةٌ مِنَ الثَّانِيَةِ -يَعْنِي الْأَرْضَ الثانية -فلما أراد الله أن يهلك عادا، أَمَرَ خَازِنَ الرِّيحِ أَنْ يُرْسِلَ عَلَيْهِمْ رِيحًا تُهْلِكُ عَادًا، فَقَالَ: يَا رَبِّ، أُرْسِلُ عَلَيْهِمْ من الريح قدر منخر الثور. قال له الْجَبَّارُ تَبَارَكَ وَتَعَالَى: لَا إِذًا تَكْفَأُ الْأَرْضَ وما عليها، وَلَكِنْ أَرْسِلْ عَلَيْهِمْ بِقَدْرِ خَاتَمٍ"، فَهِيَ الَّتِي قَالَ اللَّهُ فِي كِتَابِهِ: ﴿مَا تَذَرُ مِنْ شَيْءٍ أَتَتْ عَلَيْهِ إِلا جَعَلَتْهُ كَالرَّمِيمِ﴾ [الذَّرِايَاتِ: ٤٢] . هَذَا حَدِيثٌ غَرِيبٌ، وَرَفْعُهُ مُنْكَرٌ. وَالْأَظْهَرُ أَنَّهُ مِنْ كَلَامِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمْرٍو، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ.

---

## 30:52-53 — verses 52-53 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says: just as it is not within your power to make the dead in their graves hear, nor to make your speech reach the deaf who cannot hear, and who are, in addition, turning away from you, likewise you are not able to guide the blind away from the truth or turn them back from their error. Rather, that belongs to God, the Almighty. For He, by His power, makes the dead hear the voices of the living when He wills, and He guides whom He wills and leads astray whom He wills, and that belongs to no one besides Him. This is why He said: {You can only make hear those who believe in Our signs, and they are submitting}, meaning: submissive, responsive, obedient. Those are the ones who listen to the truth and follow it, and this is the state of the believers, while the former is the likeness of the disbelievers, as the Almighty said: {Only those who hear will respond. As for the dead, God will resurrect them, then to Him they will be returned} [al-An'am: 36].

The Mother of the Believers, A'isha, may God be pleased with her, used this verse, {You cannot make the dead hear}, as evidence that Abdullah ibn Umar was mistaken in his report that the Prophet ﷺ addressed the slain who had been thrown into the well of Badr three days later, rebuking them and reproaching them, until Umar said to him: "O Messenger of God, why do you address a people who have already rotted?" He said: "By the One in whose hand is my soul, you do not hear what I say better than they do, but they cannot respond." A'isha interpreted this by saying that he actually said: "They now know that what I used to tell them was true."

Qatada said: God brought them back to life for him so that they heard his words as a rebuke, a reproach, and a punishment.

The correct view among the scholars is the report of Ibn Umar, because it has many corroborating witnesses to its soundness from numerous angles. The most famous of these is what Ibn Abd al-Barr related, deeming it sound, from Ibn Abbas, as a raised report (marfu'): "There is no one who passes by the grave of his Muslim brother whom he knew in this world, and greets him with salam, except that God restores his spirit to him so that he returns the greeting."

[It is firmly established from him ﷺ that the deceased hears the sound of the sandals of those who accompanied his funeral when they turn away from him. The Prophet ﷺ prescribed for his nation that when they greet the people of the graves, they should greet them with the greeting of one addressing someone present, so the Muslim says: "Peace be upon you, abode of a believing people." This is an address to one who hears and comprehends, and were it not for this address, they would be in the position of addressing something nonexistent or an inanimate object. The predecessors are unanimous on this. Numerous reports (mutawatir) have come down from them that the dead recognizes the visit of the living to him and rejoices at it. Ibn Abi al-Dunya related in the Book of Graves, from A'isha, may God be pleased with her, that she said: The Messenger of God ﷺ said: "There is no man who visits the grave of his brother and sits by it except that the deceased feels companionship with him and returns his greeting until he rises to leave."

It was related from Abu Hurayrah, may God be pleased with him, that he said: When a man passes by a grave he recognizes and greets it, the greeting is returned to him.

Ibn Abi al-Dunya related with his chain from a man of the family of Asim al-Jahdari who said: I saw Asim al-Jahdari in my dream two years after his death, and I said: "Are you not dead?" He said: "Yes indeed." I said: "Then where are you?" He said: "I am, by God, in a garden among the gardens of Paradise, I and a group of my companions gather every Friday night and its morning with Bakr ibn Abdullah al-Muzani, and we receive news of you." I said: "Are your bodies present, or your spirits?" He said: "Far from it! The bodies have decayed; it is only the spirits that meet." I said: "Do you know of our visits to you?" He said: "We know of it on Friday evening, throughout the day of Friday, and on Saturday until sunrise." I said: "Why is that, rather than all the other days?" He said: "Because of the excellence and greatness of the day of Friday."

He said: Muhammad ibn al-Husayn related to us, Bakr ibn Muhammad related to us, Hasan al-Qassab said: I used to go out with Muhammad ibn Wasi' every Saturday morning until we reached the people of the cemetery, and we would stand at the graves and greet them and pray for them, then we would leave. One day I said: "What if I made this day Monday instead?" He said: "It has reached me that the dead know of their visitors on Friday, and the day before it, and the day after it." He said: Muhammad related to us, Abd al-Aziz ibn Aban related to us, he said: Sufyan al-Thawri related to us, he said: It reached me from al-Dahhak that he said: "Whoever visits a grave on Saturday before sunrise, the deceased knows of his visit." He was asked: "How is that?" He said: "Because of the position of the day of Friday."

Khalid ibn Khidash related to us, Ja'far ibn Sulayman related to us, from Abu al-Tayyah who said: Mutarrif used to go out early, and when it was Friday he would travel by night. He said: And I heard Abu al-Tayyah say: It reached us that he used to stay in a low-lying area, and one night he came, and when he was at the graves he stopped while on his horse, and he saw the people of the graves, each grave's occupant sitting upon his grave. They said: "This is Mutarrif, who comes for Friday." [Someone asked:] "Do they pray at your place on the day of Friday?" They said: "Yes, and we know what the birds say about it." I said: "What do they say?" He said: "They say, peace be upon you." Muhammad ibn al-Hasan related to me, Yahya ibn Abi Bakr related to us, al-Fadl ibn al-Muwaffaq, the maternal cousin of Sufyan ibn Uyayna, related to us, he said: When my father died I grieved for him severely, so I used to come to his grave every day, then I fell short of that for as long as God willed, then I came to him one day, and while I was sitting at the grave my eyes overcame me and I slept, and I saw as if my father's grave had opened, and as if he were sitting in his grave wrapped in his shrouds, with the appearance of the dead upon him. He said: It was as if I wept when I saw him. He said: "O my son, what has delayed you from me?" I said: "Do you really know of my coming?" He said: "You never came a single time without my knowing it, and you used to come to me and I would be pleased by you, and those around me would be pleased by your prayer." He said: So I used to come to him after that frequently.

Muhammad related to me, Yahya ibn Bastam related to us, Uthman ibn Suwayd al-Tufawi said, and his mother was among the devout women, and she was called "the nun" (rahiba): When she was on her deathbed she raised her head to the sky and said: "O my treasure and my reserve, the One upon whom I rely in my life and after my death, do not abandon me at death and do not leave me in fright." He said: Then she died. So I used to come to her every Friday and pray for her and seek forgiveness for her and for the people of the graves. Then I saw her one day in my sleep, and I said to her: "O my mother, how are you?" She said: "O my son, death indeed has a severe agony, and I am, praise be to God, in a praiseworthy intermediate state (barzakh) where sweet basil is spread and we rest our heads on silk brocade and thick silk until the Day of Resurrection." I said to her: "Do you have a need?" She said: "Yes." I said: "What is it?" She said: "Do not abandon what you used to do of visiting us and praying for us, for I am given good news of your coming on Friday when you set out from your family. It is said to me: 'O Rahiba, this is your son, he has come,' and I am pleased, and those around me among the dead are pleased by that."

Muhammad related to me, Muhammad ibn Abd al-Aziz ibn Sulayman related to us, Bishr ibn Mansur related to us, he said: When it was the time of the plague, there was a man who used to frequent the cemetery and attend the funeral prayers. When evening came he would stand at the graves and say: "May God grant you companionship in your loneliness, have mercy on your estrangement, overlook your wrongdoing, and accept your good deeds," not adding anything beyond these words. He said: One evening I went home to my family and did not go to the graves to pray as I used to. He said: While I was asleep, a crowd came to me, and I said: "Who are you and what do you need?" They said: "We are the people of the graves." I said: "What do you need?" They said: "You had accustomed us to a gift from you when you set off home to your family." I said: "What is it?" They said: "The prayers you used to pray." He said: I said: "I will return to that." He said: So I never abandoned it afterward.

Even more far-reaching than this is that the deceased knows of the deeds of the living among his relatives and brethren. Abdullah ibn al-Mubarak said: Thawr ibn Yazid related to me, from Ibrahim, from Ayyub, who said: The deeds of the living are displayed to the dead, and if they see something good they rejoice and are glad, and if they see something bad they say: "O God, turn him back to what is right."

Ibn Abi al-Dunya mentioned from Ahmad ibn Abi al-Hawari, who said: Muhammad, my brother, related to us, he said: Abbad ibn Abbad came to Ibrahim ibn Salih, who was governor over Palestine, and said: "Advise me." He said: "With what shall I advise you, may God set you right? It has reached me that the deeds of the living are displayed to their dead relatives, so consider what is displayed to the Messenger of God ﷺ of your deeds." Then Ibrahim wept until his beard was drenched. Ibn Abi al-Dunya said: Muhammad ibn al-Husayn related to me, Khalid ibn Amr al-Umawi related to us, Sadaqah ibn Sulayman al-Ja'fari related to us, he said: I had an ugly, wanton disposition, and my father died, so I repented and regretted what I had neglected, then I slipped into some grave error, and I saw my father in a dream, and he said: "O my son, how great was my joy in you when your deeds were displayed to us, and we would compare them to the deeds of the righteous. But this last time, I felt severe shame because of it, so do not disgrace me before those around me among the dead." He said: I used to hear him after that saying in his supplication at dawn, and he was a neighbor of mine in Kufa: "I ask You for a return in which there is no going back and no turning aside, O Rectifier of the righteous, O Guide of those who go astray, O Most Merciful of the merciful."

This is a chapter in which there are many reports from the Companions. Some of the Ansar among the relatives of Abdullah ibn Rawaha used to say: "O God, I seek refuge in You from any deed by which I would be disgraced before Abdullah ibn Rawaha." He used to say this after Abdullah was martyred.

The greeting of salam upon the dead has been prescribed, and it is impossible to greet someone who does not perceive or know of the one greeting him. The Prophet ﷺ taught his nation that when they see graves they should say: "Peace be upon you, O inhabitants of these abodes, among the believers, and we shall, God willing, join you. May God have mercy on those of us and of you who have gone before, and those who come after. We ask God for well-being for us and for you." This greeting, address, and call is directed to something that exists, that hears, is addressed, comprehends, and responds, even if the Muslim does not hear the response. And God knows best.]

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: كَمَا أَنَّكَ لَيْسَ فِي قُدْرَتِكَ أَنْ تُسْمِعَ الْأَمْوَاتَ فِي أَجْدَاثِهَا، وَلَا تُبْلِغَ كلامَك الصُّمَّ الَّذِينَ لَا يَسْمَعُونَ، وَهُمْ مَعَ ذَلِكَ مُدْبِرُون عَنْكَ، كَذَلِكَ لَا تَقْدِرُ عَلَى هِدَايَةِ الْعُمْيَانِ عَنِ الْحَقِّ، وَرَدِّهِمْ عَنْ ضَلَالَتِهِمْ، بَلْ ذَلِكَ إِلَى اللَّهِ تَعَالَى، فَإِنَّهُ بِقُدْرَتِهِ يُسْمِعُ الْأَمْوَاتَ أَصْوَاتَ الْأَحْيَاءِ إِذَا شَاءَ، وَيَهْدِي مَنْ يَشَاءُ، وَيُضِلُّ مَنْ يَشَاءُ، وَلَيْسَ ذَلِكَ لِأَحَدٍ سِوَاهُ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿إِنْ تُسْمِعُ إِلا مَنْ يُؤْمِنُ بِآيَاتِنَا فَهُمْ مُسْلِمُونَ﴾ أَيْ: خَاضِعُونَ مُسْتَجِيبُونَ مُطِيعُونَ، فَأُولَئِكَ هُمُ الَّذِينَ يَسْتَمِعُونَ الْحَقَّ وَيَتْبَعُونَهُ، وَهَذَا حَالُ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، وَالْأَوَّلُ مَثَلُ الْكَافِرِينَ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِنَّمَا يَسْتَجِيبُ الَّذِينَ يَسْمَعُونَ وَالْمَوْتَى يَبْعَثُهُمُ اللَّهُ ثُمَّ إِلَيْهِ يُرْجَعُونَ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ: ٣٦] .

وَقَدِ اسْتَدَلَّتْ أُمُّ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ عَائِشَةُ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا، بِهَذِهِ الْآيَةِ: ﴿إِنَّكَ لَا تُسْمِعُ الْمَوْتَى﴾ ، عَلَى تَوْهِيمِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عُمَرَ فِي رِوَايَتِهِ مُخَاطَبَةَ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ الْقَتْلَى الَّذِينَ أُلْقُوا فِي قَلِيب بَدْرٍ ، بَعْدَ ثَلَاثَةِ أَيَّامٍ، وَمُعَاتَبَتَهُ إِيَّاهُمْ وَتَقْرِيعَهُ لَهُمْ، حَتَّى قَالَ لَهُ عُمَرُ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، مَا تُخَاطِبُ مِنْ قَوْمٍ قَدْ جَيَّفوا؟ فَقَالَ: "وَالَّذِي نَفْسِي بِيَدِهِ، مَا أَنْتُمْ بِأَسْمَعَ لِمَا أَقُولُ مِنْهُمْ، وَلَكِنْ لَا يُجِيبُونَ". وَتَأَوَّلَتْهُ عَائِشَةُ عَلَى أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "إِنَّهُمُ الْآنَ لَيَعْلَمُونِ أَنَّ مَا كُنْتُ أَقُولُ لَهُمْ حَقٌّ" .

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: أَحْيَاهُمُ اللَّهُ لَهُ حَتَّى سَمِعُوا مَقَالَتَهُ تَقْرِيعًا وَتَوْبِيخًا وَنِقْمَةً.

وَالصَّحِيحُ عِنْدَ الْعُلَمَاءِ رِوَايَةُ ابْنِ عُمَرَ، لِمَا لَهَا مِنَ الشَّوَاهِدِ عَلَى صِحَّتِهَا مِنْ وُجُوهٍ كَثِيرَةٍ، مِنْ أَشْهَرِ ذَلِكَ مَا رَوَاهُ ابْنُ عَبْدِ الْبَرِّ مُصَحِّحًا [لَهُ] ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ مَرْفُوعًا: "مَا مِنْ أَحَدٍ يَمُرُّ بِقَبْرِ أَخِيهِ الْمُسْلِمِ، كَانَ يَعْرِفُهُ فِي الدُّنْيَا، فَيُسَلِّمُ عَلَيْهِ، إِلَّا رَدَّ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ رُوحَهُ، حَتَّى يَرُدَّ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامَ" .

[وَثَبَتَ عَنْهُ ﷺ أَنَّ الْمَيِّتَ يَسْمَعُ قَرْعَ نِعَالِ الْمُشَيِّعِينَ لَهُ، إِذَا انْصَرَفُوا عَنْهُ، وَقَدْ شَرَعَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ لِأُمَّتِهِ إِذَا سَلَّمُوا عَلَى أَهْلِ الْقُبُورِ أَنْ يُسَلِّمُوا عَلَيْهِمْ سَلَامَ مَنْ يُخَاطِبُونَهُ فَيَقُولُ الْمُسْلِمُ: السَّلَامُ عَلَيْكُمْ دَارَ قَوْمٍ مُؤْمِنِينَ، وَهَذَا خِطَابٌ لِمَنْ يَسْمَعُ وَيَعْقِلُ، وَلَوْلَا هَذَا الْخِطَابُ لَكَانُوا بِمَنْزِلَةِ خِطَابِ الْمَعْدُومِ وَالْجَمَادِ، وَالسَّلَفُ مُجْمِعُونَ عَلَى هَذَا، وَقَدْ تَوَاتَرَتِ الْآثَارُ عَنْهُمْ بِأَنَّ الْمَيِّتَ يَعْرِفُ بِزِيَارَةِ الْحَيِّ لَهُ وَيَسْتَبْشِرُ، فَرَوَى ابْنُ أَبِي الدُّنْيَا فِي كِتَابِ الْقُبُورِ عَنْ عَائِشَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا، قَالَتْ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "مَا مِنْ رَجُلٍ يَزُورُ قَبْرَ أَخِيهِ وَيَجْلِسُ عِنْدَهُ، إِلَّا اسْتَأْنَسَ بِهِ وَرَدَّ عَلَيْهِ حَتَّى يَقُومَ".

وَرُوِيَ عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: إِذَا مَرَّ رَجُلٌ بِقَبْرٍ يَعْرِفُهُ فَسَلَّمَ عَلَيْهِ، رَدَّ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامَ.

وَرَوَى ابْنُ أَبِي الدُّنْيَا بِإِسْنَادِهِ عَنْ رَجُلٍ مِنْ آلِ عَاصِمٍ الجَحْدَرِي قَالَ: رَأَيْتُ عَاصِمًا الْجَحْدَرَيَّ فِي مَنَامِي بَعْدَ مَوْتِهِ بِسَنَتَيْنِ، فَقُلْتُ: أَلَيْسَ قَدْ مِتَّ؟ قَالَ: بَلَى، قُلْتُ: فَأَيْنَ أَنْتَ؟ قَالَ: أَنَا -وَاللَّهِ -فِي رَوْضَةٍ مِنْ رِيَاضِ الْجَنَّةِ، أَنَا وَنَفَرٌ مِنْ أَصْحَابِي نَجْتَمِعُ كُلَّ لَيْلَةِ جُمْعَةٍ وَصَبِيحَتِهَا إِلَى بَكْرِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ الْمُزَنِيِّ، فَنَتَلَقَّى أَخْبَارَكُمْ. قَالَ: قُلْتُ: أَجْسَامُكُمْ أَمْ أَرْوَاحُكُمْ؟ قَالَ: هَيْهَاتَ! قَدْ بَلِيَتِ الْأَجْسَامُ، وَإِنَّمَا تَتَلَاقَى الْأَرْوَاحُ، قَالَ: قُلْتُ: فَهَلْ تَعْلَمُونَ بِزِيَارَتِنَا إِيَّاكُمْ؟ قَالَ: نَعْلَمُ بِهَا عَشِيَّةَ الْجُمْعَةِ وَيَوْمَ الْجُمْعَةِ كُلَّهُ وَيَوْمَ السَّبْتِ إِلَى طُلُوعِ الشَّمْسِ، قَالَ: قُلْتُ: فَكَيْفَ ذَلِكَ دُونَ الْأَيَّامِ كُلِّهَا؟ قَالَ: لِفَضْلِ يَوْمِ الْجُمْعَةِ وَعَظْمَتِهِ.

قَالَ: وَحَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ الْحُسَيْنِ، ثَنَا بَكْرُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ، ثَنَا حَسَنٌ الْقَصَّابُ قَالَ: كُنْتُ أَغْدُو مَعَ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ وَاسْعٍ فِي كُلِّ غَدَاةِ سَبْتٍ حَتَّى نَأْتِيَ أَهْلَ الْجَبَّانِ، فَنَقِفُ عَلَى الْقُبُورِ فَنُسَلِّمُ عَلَيْهِمْ، وَنَدْعُو لَهُمْ ثُمَّ نَنْصَرِفُ، فَقُلْتُ ذَاتَ يَوْمٍ: لَوْ صَيَّرْتُ هَذَا الْيَوْمَ يَوْمَ الِاثْنَيْنِ؟ قَالَ: بَلَغَنِي أَنَّ الْمَوْتَى يَعْلَمُونَ بِزُوَّارِهِمْ يَوْمَ الْجُمْعَةِ وَيَوْمًا قَبْلَهَا وَيَوْمًا بَعْدَهَا. قَالَ: ثَنَا مُحَمَّدٌ، ثَنَا عَبْدُ الْعَزِيزِ بْنُ أَبَانٍ قَالَ: ثَنَا سُفْيَانُ الثَّوْرِيُّ قَالَ: بَلَغَنِي عَنِ الضَّحَّاكِ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: مَنْ زَارَ قَبْرًا يَوْمَ السَّبْتِ قَبْلَ طُلُوعِ الشَّمْسِ عَلِمَ الْمَيِّتُ بِزِيَارَتِهِ، فَقِيلَ لَهُ: وَكَيْفَ ذَلِكَ؟ قَالَ: لِمَكَانِ يَوْمِ الْجُمُعَةِ.

حَدَّثَنَا خَالِدُ بْنُ خِدَاش، ثَنَا جَعْفَرُ بْنُ سُلَيْمَانَ، عَنْ أَبِي التَّيَّاح يَقُولُ: كَانَ مُطَرَّف يَغْدُو، فَإِذَا كَانَ يَوْمُ الْجُمْعَةِ أَدْلَجَ. قَالَ: وَسَمِعْتُ أَبَا الْتَّيَّاحِ يَقُولُ: بَلَغَنَا أَنَّهُ كَانَ يَنْزِلُ بِغَوْطَةٍ، فَأَقْبَلَ لَيْلَةً حَتَّى إِذَا كَانَ عِنْدَ الْمَقَابِرِ يَقُومُ وَهُوَ عَلَى فَرَسِهِ، فَرَأَى أَهْلَ الْقُبُورِ كُلَّ صَاحِبِ قَبْرٍ جَالِسًا عَلَى قَبْرِهِ، فَقَالُوا: هَذَا مُطَرِّفٌ يَأْتِي الْجُمْعَةِ وَيُصَلُّونَ عِنْدَكُمْ يَوْمَ الْجُمْعَةِ؟ قَالُوا: نَعَمْ، وَنَعْلَمُ مَا يَقُولُ فِيهِ الطَّيْرُ. قُلْتُ: وَمَا يَقُولُونَ؟ قَالَ: يَقُولُونَ سَلَامٌ عَلَيْكُمْ؛ حَدَّثَنِي مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ الْحَسَنِ، ثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ أَبِي بَكْرٍ، ثَنَا الْفَضْلُ بْنُ الْمُوَفَّقِ ابْنُ خَالِ سُفْيَانَ بْنِ عُيَيْنَةَ قَالَ: لَمَّا مَاتَ أَبِي جَزِعْتُ عَلَيْهِ جَزَعًا شَدِيدًا، فَكُنْتُ آتِي قَبْرَهُ فِي كُلِّ يَوْمٍ، ثُمَّ قَصَّرْتُ عَنْ ذَلِكَ مَا شَاءَ اللَّهُ، ثُمَّ إِنِّي أَتَيْتُهُ يَوْمًا، فَبَيْنَا أَنَا جَالِسٌ عِنْدَ الْقَبْرِ غَلَبَتْنِي عَيْنَايَ فَنِمْتُ، فَرَأَيْتُ كَأَنَّ قَبْرَ أَبِي قَدِ انْفَرَجَ، وَكَأَنَّهُ قَاعِدٌ فِي قَبْرِهِ مُتَوَشِّحٌ أَكْفَانَهُ، عَلَيْهِ سِحْنَة الْمَوْتَى، قَالَ: فَكَأَنِّي بَكَيْتُ لَمَّا رَأَيْتُهُ. قَالَ: يَا بُنَيَّ، مَا أَبْطَأَ بِكَ عَنِّي؟ قُلْتُ: وَإِنَّكَ لَتَعْلَمُ بِمَجِيئِي؟ قَالَ: مَا جِئْتَ مَرَّةً إِلَّا عَلِمْتُهَا، وَقَدْ كُنْتَ تَأْتِينِي فَأُسَرُّ بِكَ وَيُسَرُّ مِنْ حَوْلِي بِدُعَائِكَ، قَالَ: فَكُنْتُ آتِيهِ بَعْدَ ذَلِكَ كَثِيرًا.

حَدَّثَنِي مُحَمَّدٌ، حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ بَسْطام، ثَنَا عُثْمَانُ بْنُ سُوَيْد الطُّفَاوي قَالَ: وَكَانَتْ أُمُّهُ مِنَ الْعَابِدَاتِ، وَكَانَ يُقَالُ لَهَا: رَاهِبَةٌ، قَالَ: لَمَّا احْتَضَرَتْ رَفَعَتْ رَأْسَهَا إِلَى السَّمَاءِ فَقَالَتْ: يَا ذُخْرِي وَذَخِيرَتِي مَنْ عَلَيْهِ اعْتِمَادِي فِي حَيَاتِي وَبَعْدَ مَوْتِي، لَا تَخْذُلْنِي عِنْدَ الْمَوْتِ وَلَا تُوحِشْنِي. قَالَ: فَمَاتَتْ. فَكُنْتُ آتِيهَا فِي كُلِّ جُمْعَةٍ فَأَدْعُو لَهَا وَأَسْتَغْفِرُ لَهَا وَلِأَهْلِ الْقُبُورِ، فَرَأَيْتُهَا ذَاتَ يَوْمٍ فِي مَنَامِي، فَقُلْتُ لَهَا: يَا أُمِّي، كَيْفَ أَنْتِ؟ قَالَتْ: أَيْ: بُنِيَّ، إِنَّ لِلْمَوْتِ لَكُرْبَةً شَدِيدَةً، وَإِنِّي بِحَمْدِ اللَّهِ لَفِي بَرْزَخٍ مَحْمُودٍ يُفْرَشُ فِيهِ الرَّيْحَانُ، وَنَتَوَسَّدُ السُّنْدُسَ وَالْإِسْتَبْرَقَ إِلَى يَوْمِ النُّشُورِ، فَقُلْتُ لَهَا: أَلِكِ حَاجَةٌ؟ قَالَتْ: نَعَمْ، قُلْتُ: وَمَا هِيَ؟ قَالَتْ: لَا تَدَعْ مَا كُنْتَ تَصْنَعُ مِنْ زِيَارَاتِنَا وَالدُّعَاءِ لَنَا، فَإِنِّي لَأُبَشَّرُ بِمَجِيئِكَ يَوْمَ الْجُمْعَةِ إِذَا أَقْبَلْتَ مِنْ أَهْلِكَ، يُقَالُ لِي: يَا رَاهِبَةُ، هَذَا ابْنُكِ، قَدْ أَقْبَلَ، فَأُسَرَّ وَيُسَرُّ بِذَلِكَ مَنْ حَوْلِي مِنَ الْأَمْوَاتِ.

حَدَّثَنِي مُحَمَّدٌ، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَبْدِ الْعَزِيزِ بْنِ سُلَيْمَانَ، حَدَّثَنَا بِشْرُ بْنُ مَنْصُورٍ قَالَ: لَمَّا كَانَ زَمَنُ الطَّاعُونِ كَانَ رَجُلٌ يَخْتَلِفُ إِلَى الْجَبَّانِ، فَيَشْهَدُ الصَّلَاةَ عَلَى الْجَنَائِزِ، فَإِذَا أَمْسَى وَقَفَ عَلَى الْمَقَابِرِ فَقَالَ: آنَسَ اللَّهُ وَحْشَتَكُمْ، وَرَحِمَ غُرْبَتَكُمْ، وَتَجَاوَزَ عَنْ مُسِيئِكُمْ، وَقَبِلَ حَسَنَاتِكُمْ، لَا يَزِيدُ عَلَى هَؤُلَاءِ الْكَلِمَاتِ، قَالَ: فَأَمْسَيْتُ ذَاتَ لَيْلَةٍ وَانْصَرَفْتُ إِلَى أَهْلِي وَلَمْ آتِ الْمَقَابِرَ فَأَدْعُو كَمَا كُنْتُ أَدْعُو، قَالَ: فَبَيْنَا أَنَا نَائِمٌ إِذَا بِخَلْقٍ قَدْ جَاءُونِي، فَقُلْتُ: مَا أَنْتُمْ وَمَا حَاجَتُكُمْ؟ قَالُوا: نَحْنُ أَهْلُ الْمَقَابِرِ، قُلْتُ: مَا حَاجَتُكُمْ؟ قَالُوا: إِنَّكَ عَوَّدْتَنَا مِنْكَ هَدِيَّةً عِنْدَ انْصِرَافِكَ إِلَى أَهْلِكَ، قُلْتُ: وَمَا هِيَ؟ قَالُوا: الدَّعَوَاتُ الَّتِي كُنْتَ تَدْعُو بِهَا، قَالَ: قُلْتُ فَإِنِّي أَعُودُ لِذَلِكَ، قَالَ: فَمَا تَرَكْتُهَا بَعْدُ.

وَأَبْلَغُ مِنْ ذَلِكَ أَنَّ الْمَيِّتَ يَعْلَمُ بِعَمَلِ الْحَيِّ مِنْ أَقَارِبِهِ وَإِخْوَانِهِ. قَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ الْمُبَارَكِ: حَدَّثَنِي ثَوْرُ بْنُ يَزِيدَ، عَنْ إِبْرَاهِيمَ، عَنْ أَيُّوبَ قَالَ: تُعْرَضُ أَعْمَالُ الْأَحْيَاءِ عَلَى الْمَوْتَى، فَإِذَا رَأَوْا حَسَنًا فَرِحُوا وَاسْتَبْشَرُوا وَإِنْ رَأَوْا سُوءًا قَالُوا: اللَّهُمَّ رَاجِعْ بِهِ.

وَذَكَرَ ابْنُ أَبِي الدُّنْيَا عَنْ أَحْمَدَ بْنِ أَبِي الْحُوَارَى قَالَ: ثَنَا مُحَمَّدٌ أَخِي قَالَ: دَخَلَ عَبَّادُ بْنُ عَبَّادٍ عَلَى إِبْرَاهِيمَ بْنِ صَالِحٍ وَهُوَ عَلَى فِلَسْطِينَ فَقَالَ: عِظْنِي، قَالَ: بِمَ أَعِظُكَ، أَصْلَحَكَ اللَّهُ؟ بَلَغَنِي أَنَّ أَعْمَالَ الْأَحْيَاءِ تُعْرَضُ عَلَى أَقَارِبِهِمْ مِنَ الْمَوْتَى، فَانْظُرْ مَا يُعْرَضُ عَلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ مِنْ عَمَلِكَ، فَبَكَى إِبْرَاهِيمُ حَتَّى أَخْضَلَ لِحْيَتَهُ. قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي الدُّنْيَا: وَحَدَّثَنِي مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ الْحُسَيْنِ، ثَنَا خَالِدُ بْنُ عَمْرٍو الْأُمَوِيُّ، ثَنَا صَدَقَةُ بْنُ سُلَيْمَانَ الْجَعْفَرِيُّ قَالَ: كَانَتْ لِي شِرَّة سَمِجَة، فَمَاتَ أَبِي فَتُبْتُ وَنَدِمْتُ عَلَى مَا فَرَّطْتُ، ثُمَّ زَلَلْتُ أَيُّمَا زَلَّةٍ، فَرَأَيْتُ أَبِي فِي الْمَنَامِ، فَقَالَ: أَيْ بُنَيَّ، مَا كَانَ أَشَدَّ فَرَحِي بِكَ وَأَعْمَالُكَ تُعْرَضُ عَلَيْنَا، فَنُشَبِّهُهَا بِأَعْمَالِ الصَّالِحِينَ، فَلَمَّا كَانَتْ هَذِهِ الْمَرَّةُ اسْتَحْيَيْتُ لِذَلِكَ حَيَاءً شَدِيدًا، فَلَا تُخْزِنِي فِيمَنْ حَوْلِي مِنَ الْأَمْوَاتِ، قَالَ: فَكُنْتُ أَسْمَعُهُ بَعْدَ ذَلِكَ يَقُولُ فِي دُعَائِهِ فِي السَّحَرِ، وَكَانَ جَارًا لِي بِالْكُوفَةِ: أَسْأَلُكَ إِيَابَةً لَا رَجْعَةَ فِيهَا وَلَا حَوْرَ، يَا مُصْلِحَ الصَّالِحِينَ، وَيَا هَادِيَ الْمُضِلِّينَ، وَيَا أَرْحَمَ الرَّاحِمِينَ.

وَهَذَا بَابٌ فِيهِ آثَارٌ كَثِيرَةٌ عَنِ الصَّحَابَةِ. وَكَانَ بَعْضُ الْأَنْصَارِ مِنْ أَقَارِبِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ رَوَاحَةَ يَقُولُ: اللَّهُمَّ إِنِّي أَعُوذُ بِكَ مِنْ عَمَلٍ أَخْزَى بِهِ عِنْدَ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ رَوَاحَةَ، كَانَ يَقُولُ ذَلِكَ بَعْدَ أَنِ اسْتُشْهِدَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ.

وَقَدْ شُرِعَ السَّلَامُ عَلَى الْمَوْتَى، وَالسَّلَامُ عَلَى مَنْ لَمْ يَشْعُرْ وَلَا يَعْلَمُ بِالْمُسْلِمِ مُحَالٌ، وَقَدْ عَلِمَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ أُمَّتَهُ إِذَا رَأَوُا الْقُبُورَ أَنْ يَقُولُوا: "سَلَامٌ عَلَيْكُمْ أَهْلَ الدِّيَارِ مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، وَإِنَّا إِنْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ بِكُمْ لَاحِقُونَ، يَرْحَمُ اللَّهُ الْمُسْتَقْدِمِينَ مِنَّا وَمِنْكُمْ وَالْمُسْتَأْخِرِينَ، نَسْأَلُ اللَّهَ لَنَا وَلَكُمُ الْعَافِيَةَ"، فَهَذَا السَّلَامُ وَالْخِطَابُ وَالنِّدَاءُ لِمَوْجُودٍ يَسْمَعُ وَيُخَاطِبُ وَيَعْقِلُ وَيَرُدُّ، وَإِنْ لَمْ يَسْمَعِ الْمُسْلِمُ الرَّدَّ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ] .

---

## 30:54 — verse 54

### Translation

God, exalted is He, draws attention to the movement of the human being through the stages of creation, one state after another. His origin is from dust, then from a sperm-drop, then from a clinging clot, then from a lump of flesh. Then he becomes bones, then he is clothed with flesh, and the spirit is breathed into him. Then he comes out of his mother's womb weak, frail, of feeble strength. Then he grows little by little until he becomes a small child, then a youth, then one approaching maturity, then a young man. That is strength after weakness. Then he begins to decline, so he reaches middle age, then he grows old, then he reaches decrepit old age. That is weakness after strength. His resolve, his movement, and his physical power weaken, the hair of his temples turns white, and his outward and inward attributes change. For this reason He said: {Then He ordains weakness and grey hair after strength. He creates what He wills}, meaning: He does what He wills and disposes of His servants as He wishes, {and He is the All-Knowing, the All-Powerful}.

Imam Ahmad said: Waki' related to us, from Fudayl and Yazid, Fudayl ibn Marzuq related to us, from Atiyyah al-Awfi, who said: I recited to Ibn Umar: {God is the One who created you from weakness, then made after weakness strength, then made after strength weakness}. He said: {God is the One who created you from weakness, then made after weakness strength, then made after strength weakness}. Then he said: I recited to the Messenger of God ﷺ just as you have recited to me, and he took a pledge from me just as I have taken a pledge from you.

Abu Dawud and al-Tirmidhi related it, and al-Tirmidhi deemed it hasan (sound), from the hadith of Fudayl, with this chain. Abu Dawud also related it from the hadith of Abdullah ibn Jabir, from Atiyyah, from Abu Sa'id, in similar wording.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُنَبِّهُ تَعَالَى عَلَى تَنَقُّلِ الْإِنْسَانِ فِي أَطْوَارِ الْخَلْقِ حَالًا بَعْدَ حَالٍ، فَأَصْلُهُ مِنْ تُرَابٍ، ثُمَّ مِنْ نُطْفَةٍ، ثُمَّ مِنْ عَلَقَةٍ، ثُمَّ مِنْ مُضْغَةٍ، ثُمَّ يَصِيرُ عِظَامًا ثُمَّ يُكسَى لَحْمًا، ويُنفَخ فِيهِ الرُّوحُ، ثُمَّ يَخْرُجُ مِنْ بَطْنِ أُمِّهِ ضَعِيفًا نَحِيفًا وَاهِنَ الْقُوَى. ثُمَّ يَشِبُّ قَلِيلًا قَلِيلًا حَتَّى يَكُونَ صَغِيرًا، ثُمَّ حَدَثا، ثُمَّ مُرَاهِقًا، ثُمَّ شَابًّا. وَهُوَ الْقُوَّةُ بَعْدَ الضَّعْفِ، ثُمَّ يَشْرَعُ فِي النَّقْصِ فَيَكْتَهِلُ ، ثُمَّ يَشِيخُ ثُمَّ يَهْرَمُ، وَهُوَ الضَّعْفُ بَعْدَ الْقُوَّةِ. فَتَضْعُفُ الْهِمَّةُ وَالْحَرَكَةُ وَالْبَطْشُ، وَتَشِيبُ اللّمَّة، وَتَتَغَيَّرُ الصِّفَاتُ الظَّاهِرَةُ وَالْبَاطِنَةُ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿ثُمَّ جَعَلَ مِنْ بَعْدِ قُوَّةٍ ضَعْفًا وَشَيْبَةً يَخْلُقُ مَا يَشَاءُ﴾ أَيْ: يَفْعَلُ مَا يَشَاءُ وَيَتَصَرَّفُ فِي عَبِيدِهِ بِمَا يُرِيدُ، ﴿وَهُوَ الْعَلِيمُ الْقَدِيرُ﴾ .

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا وَكِيع، عَنْ فُضَيْلٍ وَيَزِيدَ، حَدَّثَنَا فُضَيْلُ بْنُ مَرْزُوقٍ ، عَنْ عَطِيَّةَ الْعَوْفِيِّ، قَالَ: قَرَأْتُ عَلَى ابْنِ عُمَرَ: ﴿اللَّهُ الَّذِي خَلَقَكُمْ مِنْ ضَعْفٍ ثُمَّ جَعَلَ مِنْ بَعْدِ ضَعْفٍ قُوَّةً ثُمَّ جَعَلَ مِنْ بَعْدِ قُوَّةٍ ضَعْفًا﴾ ، فَقَالَ: ﴿اللَّهُ الَّذِي خَلَقَكُمْ مِنْ ضَعْفٍ ثُمَّ جَعَلَ مِنْ بَعْدِ ضَعْفٍ قُوَّةً ثُمَّ جَعَلَ مِنْ بَعْدِ قُوَّةٍ ضَعْفًا﴾ ، ثُمَّ قَالَ: قرأتُ عَلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ كَمَا قَرَأْتَ عَلَيَّ، فَأَخَذَ عَلَيَّ كَمَا أخذتُ عَلَيْكَ.

وَرَوَاهُ أَبُو دَاوُدَ وَالتِّرْمِذِيُّ -وحَسَّنه -مِنْ حَدِيثِ فُضَيْلٍ، بِهِ . وَرَوَاهُ أَبُو دَاوُدَ مِنْ حَدِيثِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ جَابِرٍ، عَنْ عَطِيَّةَ، عَنْ أَبِي سعيد، بنحوه .

---

## 30:55-57 — verses 55-57 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty informs of the ignorance of the disbelievers in this world and the Hereafter. In this world they did what they did of worshipping idols, and in the Hereafter a great ignorance also occurs from them. Among it is their swearing by Allah that they remained in this world only a single hour. Their purpose in that is to prevent the proof from being established against them, and to claim that they were not given respite so that an excuse could be presented to them. Allah the Almighty said: {Thus were they used to being deluded. And those who were given knowledge and faith said, "You have indeed remained, according to the Book of Allah, until the Day of Resurrection"}. That is, the believing scholars respond to them in the Hereafter just as they established the proof of Allah against them in this world. They say to them, when they swear that they remained only an hour: {"You have indeed remained, according to the Book of Allah"}, meaning in the record of deeds, {"until the Day of Resurrection"}, meaning from the day you were created until the day you were resurrected, {"but you did not know"}.

Allah the Almighty said: {So that Day}, meaning the Day of Resurrection, {no excuse of theirs will benefit those who wronged}, meaning their apology for what they did will not benefit them, {nor will they be allowed to please Allah}, meaning nor will they be returned to this world, as the Almighty said: {And if they seek to please Him, they will not be of those who are allowed to please Him} [Fussilat: 24].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنْ جَهْلِ الْكُفَّارِ فِي الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ، فَفِي الدُّنْيَا فَعَلُوا مَا فَعَلُوا مِنْ عِبَادَةِ الْأَوْثَانِ، وَفِي الْآخِرَةِ يَكُونُ مِنْهُمْ جَهْلٌ عَظِيمٌ أَيْضًا، فَمِنْهُ إِقْسَامُهُمْ بِاللَّهِ أَنَّهُمْ مَا لَبِثُوا فِي الدُّنْيَا إِلَّا سَاعَةً وَاحِدَةً، وَمَقْصُودُهُمْ هُمْ بِذَلِكَ عَدَمُ قِيَامِ الْحُجَّةِ عَلَيْهِمْ، وَأَنَّهُمْ لَمْ يُنْظَروا حَتَّى يُعذَر إِلَيْهِمْ. قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿كَذَلِكَ كَانٌوا يُؤْفَكُون. وَقَالَ الَّذِينَ أُوتُوا الْعِلْمَ وَالإيمَانَ لَقَدْ لَبِثْتُمْ فِي كِتَابِ اللَّهِ إِلَى يَوْمِ الْبَعْثِ﴾ أَيْ: فَيَرُدُّ عَلَيْهِمُ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ الْعُلَمَاءُ فِي الْآخِرَةِ، كَمَا أَقَامُوا عَلَيْهِمْ حُجَّةَ اللَّهِ فِي الدُّنْيَا، فَيَقُولُونَ لَهُمْ حِينَ يَحْلِفُونَ مَا لَبِثُوا غَيْرَ سَاعَةٍ: ﴿لَقَدْ لَبِثْتُمْ فِي كِتَابِ اللَّهِ﴾ أَيْ: فِي كِتَابِ الْأَعْمَالِ، ﴿إِلَى يَوْمِ الْبَعْثِ﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ يَوْمِ خُلِقْتُمْ إِلَى أَنْ بُعِثْتُمْ، ﴿وَلَكِنَّكُمْ كُنْتُمْ لَا تَعْلَمُونَ﴾ .

قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَيَوْمَئِذٍ﴾ أَيْ: يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، ﴿لَا يَنْفَعُ الَّذِينَ ظَلَمُوا مَعْذِرَتُهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: [لَا يَنْفَعُهُمْ] اعْتِذَارُهُمْ عَمَّا فَعَلُوا، ﴿وَلا هُمْ يُسْتَعْتَبُونَ﴾ أَيْ: وَلَا هُمْ يَرْجِعُونَ إِلَى الدُّنْيَا، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَإِنْ يَسْتَعْتِبُوا فَمَا هُمْ مِنَ الْمُعْتَبِينَ﴾ [فُصِّلَتْ: ٢٤] .

---

## 30:58-60 — verses 58-60 (shared commentary)

### Translation

God Most High says: {And indeed We have set forth for mankind in this Qur'an every kind of parable} that is, We have made the truth clear to them, We have explained it plainly to them, and We have set forth for them in it parables so that they might discern the truth and follow it. {And if you bring them a sign, those who disbelieve will surely say, "You are but falsifiers"} that is, whatever sign they might see, whether it be one they themselves demanded or another, they would not believe in it, and they would maintain that it was sorcery and falsehood, just as they said concerning the splitting of the moon and similar events. As God Most High says: {Indeed, those against whom the word of your Lord has been justified will not believe, even if every sign came to them, until they see the painful punishment} [Yunus: 96-97]. For this reason He says here: {Thus does God seal the hearts of those who do not know. So be patient, indeed the promise of God is true} that is, be patient in the face of their opposition and stubbornness, for God Most High will surely fulfill for you what He has promised you of His support for you, and His making the final outcome yours and that of those who follow you, in this world and the next. {And let not those who have no certainty make you feel unsettled} that is, rather remain firm upon what God has sent you with, for it is the truth in which there is no doubt, and do not turn away from it, for there is no guidance to be followed in anything besides it. Rather, all truth is confined within it.

Sa'id reported from Qatadah: A man from the Kharijites called out to Ali, may God be pleased with him, while he was in prayer, the dawn prayer, and said: {And it has certainly been revealed to you and to those before you: if you associate partners with God, your deeds will surely be nullified and you will surely be among the losers} [al-Zumar: 65]. Ali listened quietly to him until he understood what he said, then answered him while still in prayer: {So be patient, indeed the promise of God is true, and let not those who have no certainty make you feel unsettled}. Reported by Ibn Jarir and Ibn Abi Hatim. Ibn Jarir also reported it through another route, saying:

[chain] Ibn Waki', from Yahya ibn Adam, from Sharik, from Uthman ibn Abi Zur'ah, from Ali ibn Rabi'ah, who said: A man from the Kharijites called out to Ali while he was in the dawn prayer, and said: {And it has certainly been revealed to you and to those before you: if you associate partners with God, your deeds will surely be nullified and you will surely be among the losers}. Ali answered him while still in prayer: {So be patient, indeed the promise of God is true, and let not those who have no certainty make you feel unsettled}.

Another route: Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] my father, from Ali ibn al-Ja'd, from Sharik, from Imran ibn Zabyan, from Abu Tahya, who said: Ali, may God be pleased with him, performed the dawn prayer, and a man from the Kharijites called out to him: {If you associate partners with God, your deeds will surely be nullified and you will surely be among the losers}. Ali answered him while still in prayer: {So be patient, indeed the promise of God is true, and let not those who have no certainty make you feel unsettled}.

[What has been reported concerning the merit of this noble surah and the recommendation of reciting it in the dawn prayer]:

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Muhammad ibn Ja'far, from Shu'bah, from Abd al-Malik ibn Umayr, who said, I heard Shabib, Abu Rawh, narrating from a man among the companions of the Prophet ﷺ, that the Messenger of God ﷺ led them in the dawn prayer and recited in it surah al-Rum, and became confused in it. He said: "Indeed the Qur'an is being obscured for us, for there are people among you who pray with us and do not perform ablution properly. So whoever attends the prayer with us should perform his ablution properly."

This is a sound (hasan) chain and a sound (hasan) text, and in it lies a remarkable secret and a strange piece of news, namely that he, peace be upon him, was affected by the deficiency in the ablution of one who was praying behind him following his lead. This indicates that the prayer of the one following (the imam) is connected to the prayer of the imam.

[End of the commentary on Surat al-Rum].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَقَدْ ضَرَبْنَا لِلنَّاسِ فِي هَذَا الْقُرْآنِ مِنْ كُلِّ مَثَلٍ﴾ أَيْ: قَدْ بَيَّنَّا لَهُمُ الْحَقَّ، وَوَضَّحْنَاهُ لَهُمْ، وَضَرَبْنَا لَهُمْ فِيهِ الْأَمْثَالَ لِيَتَبَيَّنُوا الْحَقَّ وَيَتَّبِعُوهُ. ﴿وَلَئِنْ جِئْتَهُمْ بِآيَةٍ لَيَقُولَنَّ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا إِنْ أَنْتُمْ إِلا مُبْطِلُونَ﴾ أَيْ: لَوْ رَأَوْا أَيَّ آيَةٍ كَانَتْ، سَوَاءً كَانَتْ بِاقْتِرَاحِهِمْ أَوْ غَيْرِهِ، لَا يُؤْمِنُونَ بِهَا، وَيَعْتَقِدُونَ أَنَّهَا سِحْرٌ وَبَاطِلٌ، كَمَا قَالُوا فِي انْشِقَاقِ الْقَمَرِ وَنَحْوِهِ، كَمَا قَالَ [اللَّهُ] تَعَالَى: ﴿إِنَّ الَّذِينَ حَقَّتْ عَلَيْهِمْ كَلِمَةُ رَبِّكَ لَا يُؤْمِنُونَ. وَلَوْ جَاءَتْهُمْ كُلُّ آيَةٍ حَتَّى يَرَوُا الْعَذَابَ الألِيمَ﴾ [يُونُسَ: ٩٦، ٩٧] ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ هَاهُنَا: ﴿كَذَلِكَ يَطْبَعُ اللَّهُ عَلَى قُلُوبِ الَّذِينَ لَا يَعْلَمُونَ. فَاصْبِرْ إِنَّ وَعْدَ اللَّهِ حَقٌّ﴾ أَيِ: اصْبِرْ عَلَى مُخَالَفَتِهِمْ وَعِنَادِهِمْ، فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ تَعَالَى مُنْجِزٌ لَكَ مَا وَعَدَكَ مِنْ نَصْرِهِ إِيَّاكَ، وَجَعْلِهِ الْعَاقِبَةَ لَكَ وَلِمَنِ اتَّبَعَكَ فِي الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ، ﴿وَلا يَسْتَخِفَّنَّكَ الَّذِينَ لَا يُوقِنُونَ﴾ أَيْ: بَلِ اثْبُتْ عَلَى مَا بَعَثَكَ اللَّهُ بِهِ، فَإِنَّهُ الْحَقُّ الَّذِي لَا مِرْيَةَ فِيهِ، وَلَا تَعْدِلْ عَنْهُ وَلَيْسَ فِيمَا سِوَاهُ هُدَى يُتَّبَعُ، بَلِ الْحَقُّ كُلُّهُ مُنْحَصِرٌ فِيهِ.

قَالَ سَعِيدٌ عَنْ قَتَادَةَ: نَادَى رَجُلٌ مِنَ الْخَوَارِجِ عَلِيًّا، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، وَهُوَ فِي الصَّلَاةِ -صلاة الْغَدَاةِ -فَقَالَ: ﴿وَلَقَدْ أُوحِيَ إِلَيْكَ وَإِلَى الَّذِينَ مِنْ قَبْلِكَ لَئِنْ أَشْرَكْتَ لَيَحْبَطَنَّ عَمَلُكَ وَلَتَكُونَنَّ مِنَ الْخَاسِرِينَ﴾ [الزُّمَرِ: ٦٥] ، فَأَنْصَتَ لَهُ عَلِيٌّ حَتَّى فَهِمَ مَا قَالَ، فَأَجَابَهُ وَهُوَ فِي الصَّلَاةِ: ﴿فَاصْبِرْ إِنَّ وَعْدَ اللَّهِ حَقٌّ وَلا يَسْتَخِفَّنَّكَ الَّذِينَ لَا يُوقِنُونَ﴾ . رَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، وَابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ. وَقَدْ رَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ مِنْ وَجْهٍ آخَرَ فَقَالَ:

حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ وَكِيع، حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ آدَمَ، عَنْ شَرِيك، عَنْ عُثْمَانَ بْنِ أَبِي زُرْعَة، عَنْ عَلِيِّ بْنِ رَبِيعَةَ قَالَ: نَادَى رَجُلٌ مِنَ الْخَوَارِجِ عَلِيًّا وَهُوَ فِي صَلَاةِ الْفَجْرِ، فَقَالَ: ﴿وَلَقَدْ أُوحِيَ إِلَيْكَ وَإِلَى الَّذِينَ مِنْ قَبْلِكَ لَئِنْ أَشْرَكْتَ لَيَحْبَطَنَّ عَمَلُكَ وَلَتَكُونَنَّ مِنَ الْخَاسِرِينَ﴾ ، فَأَجَابَهُ عَلِيٌّ وَهُوَ فِي الصَّلَاةِ: ﴿فَاصْبِرْ إِنَّ وَعْدَ اللَّهِ حَقٌّ وَلا يَسْتَخِفَّنَّكَ الَّذِينَ لَا يُوقِنُونَ﴾ .

طَرِيقٌ أُخْرَى: قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ الجَعْد، أَخْبَرَنَا شَرِيكٌ، عَنْ عِمْرَانَ بْنِ ظَبْيان، عَنْ أَبِي تَحْيَا قَالَ: صَلَّى عَلِيٌّ رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، صَلَاةَ الْفَجْرِ، فَنَادَاهُ رَجُلٌ مِنَ الْخَوَارِجِ: ﴿لَئِنْ أَشْرَكْتَ لَيَحْبَطَنَّ عَمَلُكَ وَلَتَكُونَنَّ مِنَ الْخَاسِرِينَ﴾ ، فَأَجَابَهُ عَلِيٌّ ، وَهُوَ فِي الصَّلَاةِ: ﴿فَاصْبِرْ إِنَّ وَعْدَ اللَّهِ حَقٌّ وَلا يَسْتَخِفَّنَّكَ الَّذِينَ لَا يُوقِنُونَ﴾ .

[مَا رُوِيَ فِي فَضْلِ هَذِهِ السُّورَةِ الشَّرِيفَةِ، وَاسْتِحْبَابِ قِرَاءَتِهَا فِي الْفَجْرِ] :

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ جَعْفَرٍ، عَنْ شُعْبَةَ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الْمَلِكِ بْنِ عُمَيْرٍ، سمعت شبيب -أَبَا رَوْحٍ -يحدِّث عَنْ رَجُلٍ مِنْ أَصْحَابِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ، أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ صَلَّى بِهِمُ الصُّبْحَ، فَقَرَأَ فِيهَا الرُّومُ فَأُوهِمَ، فَقَالَ: "إِنَّهُ يُلَبَّسُ عَلَيْنَا الْقُرْآنُ، فَإِنَّ أَقْوَامًا مِنْكُمْ يُصَلُّونَ مَعَنَا لَا يُحْسِنُونَ الْوُضُوءَ، فَمَنْ شَهِدَ الصَّلَاةَ مَعَنَا فَلْيُحْسِنِ الْوُضُوءَ" .

وَهَذَا إِسْنَادٌ حَسَنٌ وَمَتْنٌ حَسَنٌ وَفِيهِ سِرٌّ عَجِيبٌ، وَنَبَأٌ غَرِيبٌ، وَهُوَ أَنَّهُ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ تَأَثَّرَ بِنُقْصَانِ وُضُوءِ مَنِ ائْتَمَّ بِهِ، فَدَلَّ ذَلِكَ أَنَّ صَلَاةَ الْمَأْمُومِ مُتَعَلِّقَةٌ بِصَلَاةِ الْإِمَامِ.

[آخِرُ تَفْسِيرِ سُورَةِ "الرُّومِ"] . _

---
